# PROGRESS-HISTORY.md — KhundiConnect full build history (archive)

> This is the append-only long-form record split out of PROGRESS.md. Newest archived entries first. The live SHORT tracker is PROGRESS.md. Do not delete entries here — this is the state-recovery record.

---

- **Current build-step:** **56 — Dynamic filter engine** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode; presentation + read, NO schema/RLS/permission change).** branch `feat/56-filter-engine-v31` (off `staging` head after 54+55); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (new shared subsystem, reused by the audience builder at build-step 78). spec `specs/56-filter-engine-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md`. tests **1199/1199** (148 suites; +17 from the new `apps/api/src/ui/filter-engine.spec.ts`). **Tenant isolation ➖** (no data-model change; the server path only NARROWS within the existing tenant-scoped list endpoint — a filter param can never widen beyond the tenant since RLS + the endpoint's where-clause bound it).
  - **What shipped (spec 56):** a reusable, framework-agnostic **filter engine** in `@kc/shared` + a web **`<FilterBar>`** integrated into `<DataList>`, with **auto client-vs-server by row-count** and **debounced** text search. The filter STATE is the serializable `FilterState` (`Record<field, FilterValue>`) — the SAME shape the custom audience builder (build-step 78) will persist as a segment.
  - **Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`, after `resolveListView`):** new types `FilterType` (`select|multiselect|boolean|numberRange|dateRange|text`), `FilterOption`, `FilterSpec` (`field/label/type/options?/labelDomain?`), `ListFilterConfig` (`listKey/filters/clientRowCap?`, default cap `DEFAULT_CLIENT_ROW_CAP = 500`), `FilterRange`, `FilterDateRange`, `FilterValue`, `FilterState`. PURE helpers: `isActiveFilterValue`, `activeFilterCount`, `normalizeForMatch` (lowercase/trim/collapse-ws), `applyFilters(rows, config, state, accessor)` (AND across active fields; fuzzy text = normalized substring; select exact; multiselect membership; boolean true/false; numberRange + dateRange inclusive bounds; ISO dates compared on the date part so a `…THH:mm` value still falls inside a `yyyy-mm-dd` bound), `filtersToQuery(state)` / `queryToFilters(query, config)` (round-trip serialization: string→`field`, array→`field=v1,v2`, boolean→`field=true|false`, range→`field_min`/`field_max`, date→`field_from`/`field_to`; empty/inactive omitted), `shouldFilterServerSide(config, total)` (`total > cap`).
  - **Web — NEW `apps/web/app/ui/filter-bar.tsx`:** collapsible "Filters (N)" accordion; one control per `FilterSpec` (text → 300ms-debounced `<Input>`; select → `<SearchSelect>`; multiselect → `<MultiSearchSelect>`; boolean → `<CheckboxRow>` "only X"; numberRange → two number `<Input>`s; dateRange → two `<DateField>`s). Active filters always render as removable chips + "Clear all" (even when collapsed). Option labels route through `formatLabel` when `labelDomain` is set (no raw enum). Logical CSS only; RTL-ready.
  - **Web — `apps/web/app/ui/data-list.tsx`:** new props `filterConfig?`, `getFilterValue?(row,field)`, `onServerFilter?(query)`, `totalRowCount?`. Internal `filterState`; `serverSide = shouldFilterServerSide(config, totalRowCount ?? rows.length)`. Client path applies `applyFilters` inside the existing `filtered` memo (after the free-text search, so they compose); server path fires a guarded effect (callback held in a ref; keyed on the serialized query) that calls `onServerFilter`. Export still exports the FILTERED set. A list with no `filterConfig` behaves exactly as before.
  - **Consumer demo — `apps/web/app/members/page.tsx`:** replaced the hand-rolled "Filters" Card with a `memberFilterConfig` (gender `select`+`labelDomain:'gender'`, status `select`+`labelDomain:'member_status'`, votingOnly `boolean`) driving the `<FilterBar>`. `getMemberFilterValue` maps fields → row values for the client path; `onMemberServerFilter` mirrors the serialized query into the existing `?gender&status&votingOnly` fetch state (which the members API already filters by) — so above `clientRowCap` the **server genuinely receives the filter query** (acceptance #2), and at/below it the roster filters in-memory. The derived **age band** stays a separate client-side `<Select>` (passed via the DataList `toolbar` slot) since it's a bucket on `age`, not a server param.
  - **i18n:** new `filters.*` keys (filters/clearAll/any/min/max/from/to/searchPlaceholder) authored in BOTH locales in `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` (`_EN`/`_UR`) + `packages/shared/i18n-deltas/filters.json`. Boolean chip shows just the filter label (no new yes/no key); reuses `common.remove`. Both i18n gates green (`i18n.spec.ts` parity + `i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts`).
  - **Gates:** `npm run typecheck` ✓ · web `npm run build` ✓ · `npm run lint` ✓ (no warnings) · `npm test -w apps/api` ✓ 1199/1199. Do-NOT-break held: free-text search, pagination, CSV export (filtered set), column resolution all unchanged.

- **Build-step 55 — Per-user column preferences** 🟢 **complete (RECOVERY ENTRY — built in a prior session that paused on a deploy timeout before its record was written; merged to `staging` and verified present here on 2026-06-27: `list_column_preference.user_id` + migration `20260709000000_user_column_prefs` are on `origin/staging`).** branch `feat/55-per-user-columns-v31`; **WORK-TYPE: FIX**. Added `userId String? @map("user_id")` (FK User SetNull) to `ListColumnPreference`; replaced the single `@@unique([tenantId, listKey])` with TWO partial-uniques via a hand-written migration (one default per `(tenant_id, list_key) WHERE user_id IS NULL`; one override per `(tenant_id, user_id, list_key) WHERE user_id IS NOT NULL`). Backend `ui.service.ts` `setMyPreference` + `PUT /ui/lists/:listKey/me` (auth-only, own pref); `getBundle` returns the caller's own overrides (`userPreferences`). Shared `resolveListColumns`/`resolveListView` gained a USER preference that wins over the Khundi default. Web header "Columns" popover (`columns-control.tsx`) writes the user override. _(Detail reconstructed from the live tree/specs; see `specs/55-*` + CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md` for the authoritative design.)_

- **Current build-step:** **53 — Census report/presentation generator + new fields + derived vulnerability + welfare-outreach view** 🟢 **complete — `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` (the v3 capstone; spec 53 designates FIXED — census data-model additions [JSON `CensusEntryData` shape] + a derived welfare-sensitive indicator → production-affecting → manual approve). NO SQL migration; census is now FACTS-ONLY (self-declared welfare flag removed), vulnerability DERIVED from facts, report deterministic, export via storage (opaque ref), outreach a human prompt (no-auto). branch `feat/53-census-report` (off `feat/52-notifications-channels`); WORK-TYPE: FEATURE. spec `specs/53-census-report.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. tests 1165/1165. ⏮️ PRIOR:** **51 — Form Builder per-instance binding + default forms** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (soft; spec 51 designates a soft `[CHECKPOINT]` — this build-step makes NO data-model / migration / RLS / `tenant_id` / permission-key / module change, it SURFACES capability that already shipped: the `census_snapshots.form_definition_id` + `prize_ceremonies.form_definition_id` soft-refs [build-steps 24/29] and the `form_definitions.is_default` column [build-step 20])** — branch `feat/51-form-binding` (off `feat/50-prize-recognition`); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (surfaces the existing form-builder per-instance binding + default as a clear, usable feature; the spec itself states Work-type FIX). spec `specs/51-form-binding.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **NO DATA-MODEL CHANGE — no new table/column/enum/migration; RLS/permissions/modules untouched.** **Behaviours:** a Census round / Prize ceremony can BIND a specific form picked by HUMAN NAME (no keys/slugs) — Census 2026 can use a different form than Census 2025; a form can be marked the per-purpose DEFAULT (`PATCH /forms/:id { isDefault }`, which clears the flag on every other form of that purpose — exactly one default per purpose, or none, enforced in the same tenant tx like one-active-per-purpose); new instances PRE-SELECT the default (editable in Pro), provisioning the shipped default on first use; a picked form is verified SAME-tenant + matching-purpose before binding (`FormsService.resolveBinding`); recognition prize categories (build-step 50) need no form. **API:** `@kc/shared` NEW `FormOptionView` (id/purpose/version/label/status/isDefault lightweight picker summary); `forms.dto` `UpdateDefinitionDto.isDefault`; `forms.service` (`updateDefinition` set/unset-default one-per-purpose, NEW `getDefaultOrActive`/`resolveBinding`/`listFormOptions`); `forms-mapper.toFormOptionView`; `census.dto` `OpenSnapshotDto.formDefinitionId`; `census.service.openSnapshot` uses `resolveBinding` + NEW `listForms`; `census.controller` NEW `GET /census/forms` (`census.view`); `prize.service.resolveCeremonyForm` → `resolveBinding` + NEW `listForms`; `prize.controller` NEW `GET /prize/forms` (`prize.view`). **Web:** `/forms` (5.88 kB) Set/Unset-default control; `/census` form-picker on the Open-census card + rebind in Round settings (Pro); `/prize` (13.1 kB) application-form picker in the ceremony modal (Pro), pre-selecting the default. **Seed:** a prior-year census round bound to a DIFFERENT (archived v2) census form than this year's — proving 2026 ≠ 2025. Gates: typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web), lint ✅ (web + api, no warnings), web build ✅ (all 33 routes), tests **1135/1135** ✅ (1123 + 12: forms.service ×7, census.service ×2 + census-v2 ×3, prize.service ×2), prisma validate ✅, seed typecheck ✅. i18n: en⇔ur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (NEW `census.formField`/`census.formPickHelp`/`prize.ceremonyForm`/`prize.ceremonyFormHelp` in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + NEW `i18n-deltas/form-binding.json`). Zero physical-direction Tailwind classes. `docs/FORM_BUILDER.md` updated. **NOTE:** no live DB/staging in the build env — RLS + binding/default semantics proven on the green forms/census/prize service specs (unit fakes) + the unchanged PGlite isolation suites; the operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots (a round/ceremony form-picker, default management, a 2025-vs-2026 different-form proof, selection by name not key, responses tied to the bound version) per the spec before promotion. **🟢 `[CHECKPOINT]` (soft) — auto-approve after 30s.** ⏭️ NEXT: build-step 52 — Notifications channels (PWA + SMS + WhatsApp, pluggable providers) (spec `specs/52-*.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`).
- **(history) build-step 50 — Prize recognition awards (Khundi-assigned, beyond academic)** ✅ **APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-26) — `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` (the spec header designates a SOFT `[CHECKPOINT]`, but this build-step CHANGES THE DATA MODEL via migration `20260707000000_prize_recognition`, so per the operator checkpoint rule — data-model change ⇒ production-affecting ⇒ manual approve — it is escalated to `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]`; "when in doubt prefer FIXED")** — branch `feat/50-prize-recognition` (off `feat/49-omj-centralize`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (NEW capability: Khundi-assigned recognition awards — most senior / most active / community service — assigned directly to an honoree with no application cycle; the FIX half broadens the build-step-29 category model with an award-kind discriminator); spec `specs/50-prize-recognition.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **DATA-MODEL CHANGE (migration `20260707000000_prize_recognition`, ADDITIVE + non-destructive over step 29):** NEW enum `PrizeAwardType` (`application_based`/`recognition`); `prize_categories` gains `award_type` (NOT NULL DEFAULT `application_based`) so every existing academic/Hifz category stays applied-for untouched. A brand-new `CREATE TYPE` may be used in the same migration's DDL (unlike `ALTER TYPE … ADD VALUE`), exactly as step 29 created+used `PrizeCategoryKind`. **RLS UNCHANGED** — `ADD COLUMN` never alters a table's Row-Level Security, so `prize_categories` keeps its build-step-29 ENABLE+FORCE `*_isolation` policy; per-tenant isolation absolute (proven on the new isolation spec). **NO new permission key** — the recognition assignment gates on the existing `prize.assign`@OWN_TENANT (it IS an assignment, not a submission); category authoring stays on `prize.approve`; no new module. **Behaviours:** a category is either `application_based` (submit → review → approve → assign, build-step 29 flow unchanged; per-instance forms from step 51 bind here) or `recognition` (the Khundi selects an honoree via `<MemberPicker>` and assigns DIRECTLY — position/title + optional gift + cash — with NO application/approval cycle, an explicit audited human act §3.5); a recognition CASH award posts the same balanced Prize expense to accounting (build-step 48); both kinds coexist in one ceremony; certificates + eligibles/announcement exports include recognition honorees (the honoree's name flows into the certificate); applying to a recognition category is REFUSED; assigning recognition under an application-based category is REFUSED. **API:** `prize.service.ts` (+`assignRecognition` on `runWithTenant` — validates recognition category + honoree, writes the entry `assigned` in one tx, posts accounting on cash; `apply()` refuses a recognition category; `createCategory`/`updateCategory` persist `awardType`), NEW `AssignRecognitionDto`, `prize.controller.ts` (+`POST /prize/recognition` `prize.assign`@OWN_TENANT), `prize-mapper.ts` (category `awardType` + application `categoryAwardType`). **Shared (`@kc/shared`):** NEW `PrizeAwardType`/`PRIZE_AWARD_TYPES`/`isPrizeAwardType`, `PrizeCategoryView.awardType`, `PrizeApplicationView.categoryAwardType`, `prize_award_type` label domain (en/ur). **Web:** `/prize` (12.8 kB) — category authoring gains an award-type selector + recognition chip; the Applications tab gains an **Assign recognition award** action (gated `prize.assign`) → a focused honoree+category+title+gift modal; the application submit category list filters to applied-for categories; recognition entries carry a Recognition badge in the list. **Seed:** a "Most Senior Member" recognition category + an assigned honoree, sitting in the same "Prize Distribution 2026" ceremony as the applied-for academic+Hifz entries. Gates: typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web), lint ✅ (web + api, no warnings), web build ✅ (all 33 routes — `/prize` 12.8 kB), tests **1123/1123** ✅ (1114 + 9 NEW: `prize.service.spec.ts` +5 — recognition assigned directly/no-cycle, recognition cash posts expense, refuse-recognition-under-applied-category, refuse-apply-to-recognition, createCategory persists awardType; NEW `prize-recognition.isolation.spec.ts` ×4 — real migration chain THROUGH step 50 on PGlite as a non-superuser: enum+column added, pre-50 category backfills to application_based, RLS preserved ENABLE+FORCE, per-tenant isolation + deny-by-default + platform-sees-all + cross-tenant insert refused). i18n: en⇔ur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (NEW `prize.*` recognition/award-type keys authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + NEW `i18n-deltas/prize-recognition.json` + `prize_award_type` label domain). Zero physical-direction Tailwind classes. `docs/PRIZE.md` updated. **NOTE:** no live DB/staging in the build env — the migration + RLS/tenant-isolation seam are proven on the green `prize-recognition.isolation.spec.ts` (real migration SQL on PGlite as a non-superuser role); the operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots (a recognition category created with no raw key; a Khundi assigns a recognition award directly to a member via the picker, no application cycle, audited; both kinds coexisting in one ceremony; a certificate for a recognition honoree; exports include both; the applied-for flow intact) per the spec before promotion. **✅ `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` — APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-26)** (data-model migration = production-affecting). ⏭️ NEXT: build-step 51 — Form Builder per-instance binding + default forms (spec `specs/51-form-binding.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`).


- **(history) build-step 46 — Storage rework: Google Drive backend + per-Khundi quota + auto-compression** ✅ **complete — `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` (hard; changes the file-storage backend + adds a new tenant-DATA table + quota enforcement → manual approve)** — branch `feat/46-storage-drive-quota` (off `feat/45-family-tree`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (Drive backend + quota + compression are NEW capability; extends `StorageService` = the FIX half); spec `specs/46-storage-drive-quota.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **DATA-MODEL CHANGE (migration `20260703000000_storage_quota_v2`, additive/non-destructive):** NEW tenant-DATA table **`storage_objects`** (the scope-agnostic usage LEDGER — one row per stored object across every upload scope; `ENABLE+FORCE` RLS `app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id=app_current_tenant_id()`, UNIQUE `(tenant_id, storage_key)`, FK→tenants CASCADE), plus nullable `tenants.storage_quota_mb` (per-Khundi cap override; NULL→default) + nullable `documents.original_size` (pre-compression bytes). **NO new permission-key / NO auth change** — reuses `settings.manage`@OWN_TENANT (tenant cap), `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS (OMJ read) + `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM (OMJ cap write). **The `StorageService` CONTRACT is stable** (presign/publicUrl unchanged for R2) so the step-39 `<FileUpload>` + step-30 doc refs are untouched. **Five parts:** **(1) ENV-selectable backend** — NEW `backends.ts`: `StorageBackend` interface + `R2Backend` (existing presign logic extracted, behaviour-identical), `GoogleDriveBackend` (service-account JWT via `node:crypto` RS256 + Drive REST via fetch, one folder per Khundi, uploads/downloads PROXIED through the API since Drive has no S3 presign), `DevBackend` (placeholder URLs), `createStorageBackend(read)` selects by `STORAGE_BACKEND` (`r2`|`gdrive`|`dev`; default r2; unknown→r2). Every backend DEV-falls-back when its creds are unset (parity with R2's existing posture). `.env.example` gains `STORAGE_BACKEND` + `GDRIVE_CLIENT_EMAIL`/`GDRIVE_PRIVATE_KEY`/`GDRIVE_ROOT_FOLDER_ID`. **(2) Per-Khundi quota** — NEW `StorageQuotaService` (RLS-scoped): used-bytes = `SUM(storage_objects.byteSize)` (computed → no running-total drift; a delete removes the row), cap = `tenants.storage_quota_mb ?? DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB` (500). `recordObject` is idempotent on the key + does the quota check + write in ONE transaction on the DELTA (a replace never counts an object's old size against itself); `assertWithinQuota` enforces on presign (declared size, UX) + commit (stored size, authoritative); `removeObject` reclaims on delete. NEW shared (`@kc/shared`): `DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB`, `MB`, `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`, `mbToBytes`/`bytesToMb`/`effectiveQuotaMb`/`wouldExceedQuota`, `storageUsageView`, `StorageBackendKind`, `StorageUsageView`, `TenantStorageUsage`. **(3) Auto-compression** — server owns the POLICY (`compressionPlanFor` → processable JPEG/PNG/WebP re-encode to WebP, cap 1600px, q0.82; SVG/GIF/PDF/non-images stored as-is) + the GUARD (`MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`) + the ACCOUNTING (`original_size` vs stored `byteSize`); because the upload is presigned DIRECT-to-storage (and the build env has no native image codec), the actual re-encode runs CLIENT-side in `<FileUpload>` via `<canvas>` (downscale + re-encode, only kept if smaller), reporting the post-compression size to the server — documented split, the same `compressionPlanFor` policy can drive a future server-side codec on the proxied Drive path without a contract change. **(4) Surfaces** — `POST /storage/commit` (record stored size, idempotent), `GET /storage/usage`, `PATCH /storage/quota` (`settings.manage`, audited), `DELETE /storage/object` (reclaim), the Drive `PUT|GET /storage/proxy` byte-proxy (key re-checked in-tenant), + NEW `StoragePlatformController` (`GET /platform/storage/usage` `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS, `PATCH /platform/storage/:tenantId/quota` `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM, both `runAsPlatform`). **Web:** Settings → Storage tab is now a real `<StorageSection>` (used/total bar, backend label, compression note, admin cap setter); the OMJ "Tenants & Modules" page gains a `<StorageCaps>` panel (per-Khundi usage + cap set); `<FileUpload>`/`<ImageUpload>` optimize→commit→reclaim (over-quota 403 → `StorageQuotaError` hint, blob reclaimed). The vault's document create/delete now record/decrement the ledger (server-side, the canonical decrement). Storage plumbing paths (`storage/upload-url`, `storage/commit`, `storage/proxy`) added to `AUDIT_SUPPRESSED_PATHS` (high-frequency churn; the meaningful `documents.upload` + `storage.set_quota` stay audited). **(5) Proof** — Gates: typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web 6/6), lint ✅ (web + api, no warnings), web build ✅ (all 33 routes; `/settings` 11.9 kB, `/platform/tenants` 4.42 kB), tests **1076/1076** ✅ (1057 + 19 NEW: `storage.isolation.spec.ts` ×8 — RLS read/insert-WITH-CHECK/delete isolation on `storage_objects`, per-Khundi SUM, replace-by-DELTA no-double-count, cap invisible cross-tenant, platform grouped usage; `storage-policy.spec.ts` ×11 — compression plan processable/as-is, quota math + boundary, usage view, backend selection + DEV fallback + live R2 presign + Drive proxy). i18n: en⇔ur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (NEW `settings.storage*`/`upload.overQuota`+`optimizing`/`platform.storage*` keys authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + `i18n-deltas/{common-ui,platform}.json`). Zero physical-direction Tailwind classes (logical `inlineSize`). **NOTE:** no live DB/Drive/staging in the build env — the abstraction + quota + compression policy + tenant isolation are proven on unit specs + the green `storage.isolation.spec.ts` (real migration SQL on PGlite as a non-superuser role); the GoogleDrive live path + the Drive proxy are STRUCTURED + DEV-fallback-safe and operator-exercised on staging (spec §38 allows proving via backend selection + DEV fallback). **Known best-effort (documented):** a member-photo/certificate REPLACE across a page reload can orphan a ledger row (client `committedKey` ref is per-mount; document delete decrements correctly server-side) — usage is recomputable from the ledger; the OMJ recompute/reconcile is future. **Operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots** (an image upload stores a compressed, dimension-reduced version — stored < original; the ref is opaque/no raw URL; used-bytes increments + a delete decrements; an over-quota upload refused with the human message; Settings → Storage shows used/total + backend; `STORAGE_BACKEND` switch r2↔gdrive; cross-tenant file read blocked) per the spec before promotion. **✅ `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` — APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-26)** (storage backend + new tenant-DATA table + quota enforcement = production-affecting). ⏭️ NEXT after approve: build-step 47 — Bereavement as its own module (spec `specs/47-*.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`). **End of v3-A.**
- **(history) build-step 45 — Family tree → modal/focused view + relationship lenses + living-arrangement overlay** ✅ **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (soft) APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-26)** — branch `feat/45-family-tree` (off `fix/44-correctness`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (re-presents the shipped tree in a focused modal = the FIX half, PLUS new relationship lenses + a living-arrangement overlay/editor = new capability); spec `specs/45-family-tree.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **NO Prisma migration / NO new table / NO RLS / NO permission-key / NO auth change** — the `households` table + `members.household_id` + the tenant-scoped, RLS-isolated households CRUD (build-step 6) ALREADY model "lives together vs separately" (members sharing a household co-reside; separate households = live apart); this step delivers the VIEW + lenses + overlay + a Pro editor that REUSES the existing, already-`members.edit`/`members.create`-gated + audited endpoints (`PATCH /members/:id {householdId}`, `POST /households`). **Five parts:** **(1) Modal/focused tree** — the family tree no longer renders inline in the roster card or the Family-Tree tab; both entry points now open a spacious `<Modal size="xl">` (`members/page.tsx`: `treeOpen`/`treeModalRoot` + `openTree(id)`), focal highlighted, click-to-refocus preserved, RTL/logical-CSS + human labels (steps 40/41). **(2) Relationship lenses** — NEW shared `RelationLens` (`both`|`birth`|`marriage`) + `familyRelationKind(relation)` (SPOUSE_OF + the attached non-Okhai-`husband` fact = MARRIAGE; every blood slot = BIRTH) + `lensIncludes(lens,kind)` — one source of truth; `family-tree.tsx` adds Both/By-birth/By-marriage chips that filter bands (By-birth hides spouse + husband-fact; By-marriage shows only spouse/husband-fact; focal always shown), marriage nodes colour-distinguished (chart-3 accent), the paternal/maternal side pivot preserved under the birth lens. **(3) Living-arrangement overlay** — NEW shared `TreeHousehold` `{id, headName, headMemberId}` + `households: TreeHousehold[]` on `FamilyTreeView`, and `householdId: string|null` on `MemberRef` (the co-residence signal); `FamilyService.getFamily` collects the DISTINCT households among the tree's member nodes (head-name labelled, RLS-scoped) via NEW `loadTreeHouseholds`; `toMemberRef` now carries `householdId`. The web overlay toggle colour-rings each node by household + draws a legend with per-household co-resident counts → two brothers in separate households read as apart, an in-law sharing one reads as living in. **(4) Pro household editor** — in the tree modal (Pro + `members.edit`-gated via `useEffectiveAccess`), a `<HouseholdEditor>` assigns the focal member to an existing household, a brand-new one (focal as head), or none — `setMemberHousehold` calls the existing audited endpoints and refetches the roster + households + tree. Read-only label when the viewer lacks `members.edit`. **(5) Seed already proves it** — `buildPlan` (build-step 6 seed) already gives each extended family TWO sons in SEPARATE households (`sonHh` per son) each with a daughter-in-law (in-law, SPOUSE_OF) living in → no seed change needed; the two-brothers-separate + in-law-co-residence cases exist for the staging screenshots. a refused delete is a 409, never this shape. **9 NEW tenant-scoped DELETE endpoints with the spec-42 decision rule + referential/immutability guards:** (1) **welfare case type** — hard-delete if unused, else ARCHIVE (`active=false`, kept for case history); (2) **welfare case** — hard-delete a pre-disbursement case, REFUSE (409) once ANY disbursement exists (disbursed welfare facts are immutable — reverse in accounting, never erase); (3) **prize ceremony** — hard-delete a draft/empty one, REFUSE if it has applications; (4) **prize category** — hard-delete if unused, else ARCHIVE; (5) **prize gift** — always a clean hard-delete (assignments copy the label as free text, no FK); (6) **prize certificate template** — hard-delete if unused, REFUSE while a ceremony links it; (7) **event** — hard-delete a draft/scheduled one with no RSVPs, REFUSE a completed event or one with RSVP/attendance (archive instead); recorded spend stays in accounting regardless (no event FK); (8) **census snapshot** — hard-delete only an empty, still-open round, REFUSE a finalized one or one with submissions; (9) **document** — hard-delete the metadata row (non-financial; blob lifecycle owned by §46). **EDIT (reuses the step-39 create modals, pre-filled, permission-gated):** events (PATCH), welfare cases (PATCH, pre-disbursement fields only — backend already restricts to open/under-inquiry), prize ceremonies (PATCH), notification templates (PUT, edit-in-place author form). Members already shipped full edit+delete (build-step 39); notification-template delete already existed (build-step 33). **NEW shared `<ConfirmDialog>` (`apps/web/app/ui/confirm-dialog.tsx`)** — built on `<Modal>` (focus-trap/ESC/scroll-lock/RTL), `danger` confirm by default, non-dismissible while busy; every destructive action routes through it (no single-click delete) and every trigger is `hasPermission`-gated (a user who can't edit/delete never sees the control). **IMMUTABILITY BOUNDARY pinned (`apps/api/src/audit/edit-delete-immutability.spec.ts`):** asserts `AccountingService` exposes NO `delete*`/`remove*` and no posted-entry update (corrections are reversing entries, §18), and `AuditService` is append-only (no delete/update on the recorder) — so a future regression that adds a delete to accounting/audit fails loudly. `permission.listTenantRoles` + `GET /access/roles` ; `StorageController` (`upload-url`/`view-url`) wired into `StorageModule`/`AppModule` ; shared `MemberSearchResult` + `TenantRoleOption` types. **Consumer conversions:** **Members** — Add/Edit → `<Modal>` (size xl, remounts per target), Photo URL field → `<ImageUpload>`, family-tree focus → `<MemberPicker>`. **Events** — Create event + Record minutes → `<Modal>` (finished the prior session's half-done conversion: state existed but no modal was rendered + the create form had been deleted). **Welfare** — Open case → `<Modal>` (subject → `<MemberPicker>`), Record death/grave → `<Modal>` (member → `<MemberPicker>`), the cramped under-inquiry view → a real completable inquiry `<Modal>`, case + bereavement document "file reference / vault key" fields → `<FileUpload>`. **Prize** — New ceremony + Submit application → `<Modal>` (applicant → `<MemberPicker>`), certificate background → `<ImageUpload>` (prior session). **Documents** — issue-card member → `<MemberPicker>`, "Restrict to roles" free-text → `<MultiSearchSelect>` of the Khundi's real roles (creatable). **Lawazim** — payer dropdown → client-side `<SearchSelect>` over the liable register (keeps the owes/clear context + year logic, scales the UI). **Branding** — removed the `https://…/logo.png` placeholder (existing upload button retained). **Census public form member-link `<select>` deliberately LEFT** (public/offline-queued submitter flow — the search picker needs `members.view` + online; documented exception). **Grep gates GREEN:** zero `members.map(... <option>)` full-roster dropdowns, zero `https://` file placeholders, zero user-facing "R2 key/Photo URL/vault key/file reference" labels (only code comments + the `<FileUpload>` doc-comment remain). **Member search never returns a CNIC** (Prisma `select` asserts lean columns only — covered by `members.service.spec.ts`). Gates: typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web), lint ✅ (web + api, no warnings), test **997/997** ✅ (993 + 4: the `members.search` lean-shape/cap/no-CNIC spec), build ✅ (all routes; `/members` 9.04 kB, `/welfare` 9.49 kB, `/events` 5.68 kB, `/prize` 10.3 kB, `/documents` 7.57 kB, `/lawazim` 7.84 kB). **NOTE:** presentation + read-endpoint build-step — no live DB/staging in the build env; the operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots (add-member modal, member autocomplete, welfare inquiry modal, role multi-select, upload-with-preview) per the spec before promotion. **🟢 `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` — awaiting manual approve.** ⏭️ NEXT after approve: build-step 40 — Enum-label sweep + de-jargon copy (spec `specs/40-label-sweep-copy.md`, CODEREF `specs/38-42-CODEREF.md`).

a partial feed never wipes a field (optional fields applied only when present); a re-fetch updates the pending row (no stacking); a local-only member is never referenced. **Corrected-model-aware (build-step 19):** the diff/merge never proposes a `member_type`/Khundi/Group-code change (those don't exist on the member); honorary/child stay DERIVED. **Secrets ✅:** the OMJ API key stays AES-GCM encrypted at rest, NEVER returned (only `hasApiKey`); the conflict comparison **masks CNIC to the last 4 on BOTH sides** (`maskCnic`) so the full national ID never reaches the wire (`omj-helpers.spec` + `omj-sync.service.spec` assert the plaintext CNIC is absent from the view). **Presentation (§34):** `/omj-sync` rebuilt on `<DataList listKey="omj_sync">` (type/status chips via the label layer, search, table↔card, export, status filter) with a field-by-field old-vs-new merge in the row's expand panel (per-field **Use OMJ / Keep current** toggles); diagnostics line (last fetch time/status + key-set badge) + Pro key management & cron note; EN/UR + RTL labels (new `omj_conflict_type`/`omj_conflict_status`/`omj_fetch_status`/`omj_match_key`/`omj_field` domains + `omjSync.*` messages). **Simple/Pro** via `useMode('omj_sync')` (registered `omj_sync` in `MODE_REGISTRY` — Simple = plain add / accept-OMJ-or-keep; Pro = per-field merge + key management + status filter). ⏭️ NEXT after approve: build-step 35 — Notifications deepen (spec `specs/35-notifications-v2.md`).

Otherwise standard isolation (tenant reads/inserts own rows; platform path reads/writes all incl. null-tenant rows; deny-by-default). `tenant_id` SET NULL on tenant delete (the trail survives, detached). **`@kc/shared`:** the audit + i18n contracts as PURE FUNCTIONS — `sanitizeAuditMetadata` (the §17 structural guarantee — any value under a sensitive key [password/token/otp/apiKey/cnic/secret/…] → `[redacted]`, recursively; strings length-capped, objects depth/breadth-capped — so a secret/PII can NEVER reach an audit row), `summarizeAuditAction` (method+route → a stable namespaced action, dropping uuid/numeric/`:param` id segments), `AUDIT_SENSITIVE_KEYS` + `AuditLogView`/`AuditPage`/`AuditActorAltitude` types; listForTenant [RLS] + listAll [platform path]); a GLOBAL `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) — the cross-cutting "audit hook" that records ONE row for every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE across EVERY module with no per-module wiring, capturing actor/action/target/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params — **never the request body**, so no credential/OTP/CNIC is ever stored); two read surfaces — `AuditController` (`/audit`, `audit.view` OWN_TENANT, RLS read — a Khundi's own trail) + `PlatformAuditController` (`/platform/audit`, `audit.view` ALL_TENANTS — OMJ/Vendor cross-tenant oversight on the audited platform path). **New permission key `audit.view` (CORE)** — OWN_TENANT for a Khundi (added to President; Deferred (noted in decisions): member self-apply/registration via the §22 PWA, PDF card printing + QR camera scanner UI, full per-request enforcement of the document `access_roles` row filter on reads (the field + `canViewDocument` helper + gate ship now). **Prior build-step 17 (now APPROVED):** **Build-step 17 essentials:** `audit_log` is the §7.11 immutable log — TENANT DATA on the §-template RLS BUT **append-only** (only SELECT+INSERT policies, NO UPDATE/DELETE → a row can never be edited/erased even by its owner tenant; proven by isolation + migration specs). `tenant_id` nullable (null = platform-level action) + SET NULL on tenant delete (trail survives detached). Rows are written by a GLOBAL `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) on every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE — **no per-module wiring** (existing module service specs untouched, all still green); it stores actor/action/target/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params — **NEVER the request body**, so no secret/CNIC/OTP is captured). `AuditService.record` is path-aware (tenant→`runWithTenant`, platform→`runAsPlatform`), re-sanitises metadata, and is NON-throwing (auditing can't break the audited action). New key `audit.view` (CORE): tenant `/audit` OWN_TENANT (President + Super Admin), cross-tenant `/platform/audit` ALL_TENANTS (OMJ Admin) / PLATFORM (Vendor). `sanitizeAuditMetadata` (shared, pure) redacts any value under a sensitive key (defense in depth). **i18n is now real, not just "RTL-ready":** `@kc/shared` `MESSAGES` EN/UR catalog + `translate` (en→key fallback) + `isRtlLocale`/`dirForLocale`; web `app/i18n.tsx` `I18nProvider` flips `<html lang/dir>` at runtime (Urdu = full RTL, no reload) + `LanguageToggle`. New shared pure fns: `summarizePlatformRevenue` (never nets collected vs outstanding; reuses `summarizeBilling` per tenant) + `censusHeatBand` (5-band heatmap classifier). **Deferred (noted in decisions):** impersonation (`tenant.impersonate` — auth-touching, a focused later step), graveyard-records view (Phase-2 `death_records`, build-step 18), a dedicated OMJ Jamat-AI-insights panel, PDF/Excel export. **Billing model:** `subscription_plans` is GLOBAL reference data (no RLS, like `permissions`); `subscriptions` + `payments` are tenant DATA (RLS, one subscription per tenant, plan FK RESTRICT, payment→subscription FK SET NULL). Money is whole-rupee Int (PKR). New keys `billing.view` (OWN_TENANT) + `billing.manage` (PLATFORM Vendor duty, in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`, ≠ tenant.manage). **White-label adds NO column** — branding is `tenants.branding` JSON + `tenants.custom_domain`; `effectiveBranding` APPLIES it ONLY when the `whitelabel` module flag is ON (else KhundiConnect defaults, retained-but-not-applied, §15.3); `GET /tenants/current` honours this. `sanitizeBranding` whitelists the §15.2 safe subset (logo/brandName/hex colors/tagline) — re-sanitized on save. `/settings/branding` is module-gated (paid → reachable; off → 404 whole surface). Module-toggle UI (`/platform/tenants`) is the build-step 5 one (unchanged) — build-step 15 added billing + branding around it. **Member portal `/me/*` is IDENTITY-gated, not permission-gated:** the service resolves the member from the AUTHENTICATED card (`user.omjCardNumber`) vs the resolved-host tenant on `runWithTenant`, so a card holder reaches only their OWN record (a non-member card → 404); `@RequireModule('portal')` still gates it (default-open). The admin `/portal/*` queue is dual-gated (`portal.requests`/`portal.suggestions`). **§22 SAFE-FIELD rule is structural:** `sanitizeProfileChanges` whitelists name/dob/education/occupation/income/contact and DROPS status/card/CNIC/member-type/gender — a member can never self-edit a constitutional field; the set is re-sanitized again at approval time. A profile change is applied to the member ONLY on an explicit admin approve (§3.5). The PWA service worker NEVER caches `/api/*` (member data + auth must stay fresh + session-scoped on a shared phone). Demo: sign in as `OMJ-JAF-0002` (OTP-only) on jafrani-b → `/me`. **Reports add NO table/migration:** they DERIVE dashboards from members/lawazim/accounting/census via the SAME shared pure functions those modules use (one source of truth — `MembersService.demographics` now also delegates to the shared `computeMemberDemographics`). The Khundi altitude reads on `runWithTenant` (RLS-isolated); the OMJ (`crossKhundi.view` ALL_TENANTS) + Vendor (`tenant.manage` PLATFORM) altitudes read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path and have NO per-tenant module gate (mirrors Vendor provisioning). The rich OMJ/Vendor dashboard UIs land with build-step 16; build-step 13 shipped the full Khundi dashboard UI + all three altitude APIs + CSV exports. After editing shared, rebuild `@kc/shared` before jest/typecheck/build (done). **AI generator SIMULATES insights unless `AI_LIVE=on`** and **messaging dispatcher SIMULATES sends unless `MESSAGING_LIVE=on`** (both optional env, default off) — so dev/staging/seed/gates never hit a provider, send PII, or bill anyone; live wiring flips the env on with real per-owner keys. **AI privacy (§11.6) is structural:** insights are built ONLY from anonymized aggregate counts (`aggregateMembersForInsight` drops names/CNIC) + `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop before any real provider call. **ai_insights RLS is a DELIBERATE widening** of the §-template — a tenant reads its own KHUNDI rows PLUS shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`), gated on a tenant context (no-context still sees nothing); writes are own-KHUNDI-only (JAMAT rows are bypass-path only). After editing the schema, **rebuild `@kc/shared` (`npm run build -w @kc/shared`) before running jest** — jest maps `@kc/shared` to its SOURCE for tests, but typecheck/build resolve the built `dist/index.d.ts`, so rebuild shared before typecheck/build when you add shared exports. PGlite UUID literals must be **hex-only** (0-9a-f) — `s`/`n` etc. are invalid. Gate infra notes: isolation + migration gates use **PGlite** (in-process Postgres/WASM, no Docker/superuser); jest needs `NODE_OPTIONS=--experimental-vm-modules` (wired into the api `test` script). Service tests use pure-function fixtures + a fake transaction client, so no live services are needed (the accounting fake must set `entryId` on nested-created journal lines so the include join resolves). After editing the schema run `npm run prisma:generate` from `apps/api` before typecheck/build (set a dummy `DATABASE_URL` for `prisma validate`/`generate`). **`nest build` gotcha: `incremental:true` + `deleteOutDir` means a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` makes tsc skip emit after dist is wiped (exit 0, empty dist) — `rm -f *.tsbuildinfo` before a clean build to verify; the turbo `npm run build` from root is the canonical build gate (it reported 3 successful).** NOTE: a stray `*/` inside a Prisma `///` doc comment will corrupt the generated client's `.d.ts` — keep doc comments clean. NOTE: `prisma/*.ts` (seed/reset) is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope and runs via `ts-node --transpile-only`; type-check it manually after edits.

| 2026-06-06 | Welfare: explicit approve→disburse, no accounting auto-post | A case is opened `open`; approve/reject/close + disburse are explicit human acts; a disbursement is REFUSED unless the case is approved/closed (`canDisburseWelfare`). `welfare_disbursements.journal_entry_id` is an OPTIONAL non-FK link — the §7.7 welfare→accounting auto-post is deferred (like the §18 lawazim→accounting auto-post), so AccountingService stays untouched + green. | confirm (defer auto-post) |
| 2026-06-06 | Death/grave is pure record-keeping (§2.6) | `death_records.deceased_member_id` is nullable + SET NULL so a record can attach to an "Okhai by birth" NON-member; graveyard name + grave number are recorded free-text (OMJ-issued — no allocation/collision logic in this software, §2.6). Seed includes one non-member grave record per tenant. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-06 | Attendance + prize assignment are explicit (§3.5) | `event_registrations.attended` is set ONLY by the `events.attendance` mark endpoint (a QR scan / manual tick) — an RSVP via `register` never marks attendance. A prize is assigned ONLY after `prize.approve` (`canAssignPrize`). Both proven by service specs (no auto-action). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-06 | Card QR carries no PII (§2.4/§17) | `buildCardQrPayload` (shared, pure) encodes `KC|{subdomain}|{omjCardNumber|NA}|{cardId}` — the canonical OMJ card number (constitutional identity, NOT a secret) + ids only; never a CNIC or any encrypted field. Derived server-side on issue (never accepted as input). Proven by helpers + `vault.service.spec`. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-06 | Document access = role-name allowlist (§7.9) | `documents.access_roles` JSON holds role NAMES; `canViewDocument(accessRoles, viewerRoleNames)` returns true when unrestricted (empty) or the viewer holds a named role. A representative role-restricted financial doc is seeded; full per-request enforcement of the row-level filter on reads is a follow-on (the field + helper + gate ship now). | confirm (filter helper) |
| 2026-06-06 | Default-role grants extended for phase-2 (§9) | President += `welfare.disburse`/`prize.{view,approve,assign}`; General Secretary += `welfare.{view,create}`/`death.{view,record}`/`events.attendance`. Other phase-2 keys were already in the seed roles (welfare.view/approve, events.*, mom.*, documents.*, cards.* on Operator). Khundi Super Admin auto-holds all. This is a permission change → part of this checkpoint. | confirm new grants |
| 2026-06-06 | Online prize/event member self-apply via PWA deferred | The `/prize` + `/events` admin surfaces ship now; member-facing self-application/registration through the §22 PWA portal (`/me`) is a follow-on. PDF/Excel card printing + a QR camera scanner UI (the camera read of the seeded payload) are also follow-ons (the payload + issue flow ship now). | confirm (defer) |
| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log` is append-only at the DB (immutable) | Per §7.11 "immutable", `audit_log` carries ENABLE+FORCE RLS with ONLY a SELECT policy + an INSERT policy — no UPDATE/DELETE policy, so those commands match nothing and are denied even to the table-owner application role. A row, once written, can never be edited or erased. Proven by `audit.isolation.spec` (owner UPDATE/DELETE affects 0 rows) + `audit.migration.spec` (`pg_policies` shows only SELECT+INSERT). `reset.ts` clears it on the bypass path for dev re-seeding only. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log.tenant_id` is nullable + SET NULL on tenant delete | A platform-level action (Vendor provisioning, OMJ cross-tenant read) has no single Khundi, so `tenant_id` is null (the §-template policy `tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()` excludes null rows from a tenant session — a Khundi never sees platform-level audit; only the bypass path does). On tenant delete the FK SET NULLs so the trail SURVIVES (detached, platform-path-only) rather than being erased — an immutable log shouldn't vanish with a tenant. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | Audit is captured by a GLOBAL interceptor, not per-module hooks | `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) records ONE row for every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE across EVERY module — the §22 cross-cutting "audit hook" with NO per-module wiring (existing module services + their specs are untouched, all 521 still green). It stores actor/action(method+route)/target(`:id` or created id)/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params) and **NEVER the request body**, so no credential/OTP/CNIC is captured (§17). Richer per-action explicit `AuditService.record` calls are an incremental follow-on. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | Interceptor altitude approximation | The interceptor sets `actor_altitude` = `tenant` when a tenant context is resolved, else `vendor` (platform host). OMJ users also operate at the platform host, so an OMJ action is recorded as `vendor` by the auto-hook; precise OMJ attribution comes from explicit `AuditService.record` calls (which take an explicit altitude) and the seeded demo rows. Acceptable for the cross-cutting default. | confirm (approximation) |
| 2026-06-06 | New key `audit.view` (CORE); tenant OWN + cross-tenant ALL_TENANTS | Added ONE permission key `audit.view` (CORE backbone, like `billing.view`). | 2026-06-06 | `sanitizeAuditMetadata` is the structural secrets guarantee | Any value under a sensitive key (password/pass/secret/token/otp/auth/credential/apiKey/api_key/key/cnic/cipher/encrypted — substring, case-insensitive) → `[redacted]`, recursively; strings/objects/arrays are length/depth/breadth-capped. Applied in the interceptor AND re-applied in `AuditService.record` (defense in depth). So §17/principle-#7 "no secret/PII in logs" holds by construction, not convention. Proven by `audit-helpers.spec` + `audit.service.spec`. | confirm reading |

| 2026-06-05 | AI generation simulates unless `AI_LIVE=on` | The `InsightGenerator` only makes a real OpenAI/Claude HTTP call when the optional `AI_LIVE` env = `on`; otherwise it SIMULATES (returns a deterministic offline insight from the same aggregate via `simulateInsight`, no network). | 2026-06-05 | AI privacy is structural (§11.6) | Insights are built ONLY from `aggregateMembersForInsight` (counts, never names/CNIC) → `buildInsightPrompt` references only the aggregate. `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop the generator calls before EVERY real provider request (throws on a CNIC/phone pattern). | 2026-06-05 | `ai_insights` RLS widened for cross-altitude visibility | Unlike the standard §-template, `ai_insights` READ = own KHUNDI rows OR shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`) — but the JAMAT clause requires a tenant context so a no-context session still sees nothing (deny-by-default). WRITE (FOR ALL) = own KHUNDI only; a tenant can never forge/modify a JAMAT row or a rival's (WITH CHECK). This implements §11.3 (Jamat insights shared downward, anonymized; never sideways). `ai_config` keeps the plain §-template (Khundi never sees OMJ's key). | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | AI Insights permission duty split | No new keys/module — the catalog already has `insights.{view,generate}` + `ai_key.manage` + module `insights`. Setting provider/model/enabled maps to `ai_key.manage` (managing the AI integration — there is no separate "insights.config" key). | 2026-06-05 | AI config = encrypted key + non-secret provider/model | The per-owner provider API key is stored as ONE AES-256-GCM ciphertext via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at generate time, never returned (`AiConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. `provider`/`model`/`enabled` are non-secret and shown in the UI. | 2026-06-05 | Provider credentials = encrypted JSON blob | The per-tenant Twilio/Infobip credentials are stored as ONE AES-256-GCM-encrypted JSON string (e.g. Twilio `{accountSid,authToken}` / Infobip `{apiKey,baseUrl}`) via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at send time. | 2026-06-05 | One double-entry engine (no "simple" data model) | Per §18, EVERY transaction — simple cashbook or detailed journal — is stored as balanced `journal_lines`. `accounting_settings.mode` is a VIEW flag only; `setMode` upserts that row and never reads/rewrites journal data (proven non-destructive by `accounting.service.spec`). The engine refuses any unbalanced/both-sided/zero entry. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cash side = a default "Cash & Bank" asset account | The double-entry cash side uses a seeded `isDefault` ASSET head ("Cash & Bank"); a line may also carry `bank_account_id` to attribute the movement to a physical bank. The cashbook = the asset-line ledger (debit=in, credit=out); opening balance = Σ `bank_accounts.opening_balance`. Keeps simple-mode auto-assignment unambiguous. | confirm |

| 2026-06-05 | Lawazim liability = voting eligibility | The §2.5 fee is "per 18+ male member". `isLawazimLiable` DELEGATES to `isVotingEligible` (active ∧ male ∧ 18+ ∧ memberType=member) so the fee population and the constitutional voting population can never drift apart; named separately so a future divergence (e.g. should an honorary ever owe) is a one-line change. | 2026-06-05 | Two independent ledgers, no money movement | The Khundi fee (income, `lawazim_payments`) and the OMJ fee (expense, `omj_remittances`) are SEPARATE. `summarizeLawazimYear` computes `collected` and `omj.remitted` from disjoint inputs and NEVER nets one against the other; the service records each independently. | 2026-06-05 | Partial payments allowed; status derived | A member may have many payments per year; standing (paid/partial/unpaid) is DERIVED by summing them vs the Khundi fee — no stored "paid" flag. | 2026-06-05 | Census permission duty split | No new permission keys/module needed — the catalog already has `census.{view,enter,approve,finalize}` + module `census`. | 2026-06-05 | Only APPROVED entries count | `summarizeCensusEntries` + the completion % count ONLY `approved` entries (§10.3 "on approval → counts in demographics"); pending/rejected never skew the roll-up. | 2026-06-05 | One entry per member per snapshot | A member has at most one entry per snapshot (a partial unique index where `member_id IS NOT NULL`); a re-submission UPDATES that row and RESETS it to `pending` (re-approval required) rather than stacking duplicates or silently keeping a stale approval. New-person entries (`member_id` null) may be many. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Below-living-wage = none/below_15k | The §10.5 below-living-wage flag is DERIVED from `incomeBand` (`isBelowLivingWage`), with the at/under-line bands = `none` + `below_15k` (coarse PKR bands `none`/`below_15k`/`15k_30k`/`30k_60k`/`above_60k`). Chosen for low-literacy entry; exact figures are never stored. | confirm bands |
| 2026-06-05 | Census progress denominator | Completion % = distinct members with an APPROVED entry ÷ total roster members. The whole roster is the denominator (simple + defensible); new-person submissions are surfaced separately and don't change the denominator. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | OMJ sync is a Khundi (tenant) feature | §22 lists "OMJ Data Sync" under **Khundi Tenant Feature Areas**, so `omj_api_config` + `fetch_conflicts` are TENANT DATA (tenant_id + §-template RLS) and the queue is per-Khundi. Each Khundi configures its own key and reviews its own conflicts; OMJ-altitude cross-tenant oversight is a later step. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cron = internal timer, not BullMQ | §4 lists BullMQ; built a dependency-free, self-rescheduling daily timer (02:00 UTC, `unref`'d, self-disables under tests/no-endpoint) so the gates need no live Redis worker. ALL per-tenant-resilient logic is in `runDailySyncAllTenants()` (what the tests exercise), so a BullMQ worker can replace the trigger later with no logic change. | confirm (vs BullMQ now) |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC matching via in-memory decrypt | CNIC is stored AES-GCM (random IV) so it can't be equality-matched in SQL. The reconcile loads the tenant's members, **decrypts CNICs in memory** (Khundis are small, §10) to build the match index; plaintext never leaves the server / is never logged. Blind-index column deferred (not needed at this scale). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Conflict dedup, not stacking | A re-fetch UPDATES the existing PENDING `fetch_conflicts` row for the same person (keyed on `local_member_id` for a conflict, else on `match_value`=cnic‖card for a `new`) rather than inserting a duplicate (§7.4). `unchanged` records are never queued. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Partial feed never wipes data | `diffIncoming` counts an OPTIONAL field as "changed" only when the OMJ record actually provides a value; `merge` likewise only overwrites fields the feed provides. A sparse feed therefore can't blank out data the Khundi holds (a silent overwrite by omission). STATUS is never changed by a merge (no silent suspend). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Resolve semantics | `accept` is valid only for a `new` record (creates a member, provenance `omj_fetch`); `merge` only for a matched `conflict` (updates the local member's identity/demographics); `reject` always valid (no member change). Wrong resolution for the type → clean 400. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | API key encryption | The per-tenant OMJ API key is encrypted at rest with the SAME AES-256-GCM field cipher as CNICs (`CnicCipherService`, key from `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, now exported from MembersModule). Never returned (`OmjConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `omj_sync` is a toggleable module | Added module key `omj_sync` (auto-included in `PROVISIONABLE_MODULES`) + keys `omj_sync.{view,config,fetch,resolve}`. Granted to Super Admin (all), General Secretary (all four), Councilor (view/fetch/resolve). | confirm new keys |
| 2026-06-05 | Voting eligibility includes `memberType=member` | §2.3's literal formula is "active ∧ male ∧ 18+". Built `isVotingEligible` as active ∧ male ∧ 18+ ∧ **memberType=member**, because §2.3 also says a `child` (even a male who turned 18) must be human-confirmed before counting and a `non_member_okhai` is "not a member". So a pending child/non-member is excluded until promoted. Computed on read (age-dependent), never stored. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Male child ≥18 → `pendingVotingActivation` flag | Derived signal (male ∧ child ∧ active ∧ ≥18) surfaced for human confirmation; the platform NEVER auto-promotes child→member or auto-counts them (§2.3, AGENT.md §3.5). Admin promotes via a normal member edit. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Tenant cannot set `suspended` | Suspension is constitutionally OMJ-altitude (§2.3; `members.suspend` is in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`). The tenant `PATCH /members/:id/status` endpoint refuses `suspended`; the OMJ oversight suspend flow lands in its own build-step. Tenants manage active/inactive/expired. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | `member_status_history` carries `tenant_id` | §7.3 sketches it without one; added `tenant_id` + the RLS template for isolation parity (no tenant-DATA table without RLS). `changed_by` is a bare actor UUID (no FK), mirroring `user_roles.assigned_by`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Family edges stored BOTH ways | Each relationship writes the edge AND its inverse (PARENT_OF↔CHILD_OF, SPOUSE_OF/SIBLING_OF symmetric) so the navigable tree (§10.2) resolves from any focal person with one "edges where from=focal" query; add/remove keep the pair in sync; unique `(tenant,from,to,type)`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC encryption | A member's CNIC is encrypted at rest with **AES-256-GCM** (`CnicCipherService`), key = SHA-256 of the existing `ENCRYPTION_KEY` placeholder (now REQUIRED at boot). Plaintext CNIC is never returned (absent from `MemberView`) or logged (§17). Reversible (vs. password hashing) because OMJ-sync matching needs it later. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `households.head_member_id` is 1:1 | Modelled head as a one-to-one (unique) relation — a member heads at most one household — so Prisma is satisfied and the head FK is unambiguous. Member delete nulls the head (SET NULL), never cascades the household. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `module_flags` is tenant DATA (has RLS) | Unlike the step-4 authz backbone (no RLS), `module_flags` carries `tenant_id` + the §-template RLS — a tenant's commercial plan must not be readable/writable by another. First tenant-DATA table to reuse the step-2 RLS template. Tenant reads its own flags via `runWithTenant` (gate + SPA menu); Vendor writes cross-tenant via `runAsPlatform`. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module default = open | `ModuleEnablementService`: `core` always on; an explicit flag row wins; a MISSING row is treated as ENABLED (default-open) — keeps the step-4 seam behaviour and means provisioning explicitly writes rows for the Vendor to toggle. Disabling is the explicit Vendor act that gates a module off. | confirm (vs default-closed) |
| 2026-06-05 | `core` never toggleable | The `core` module (auth/roles/settings) is never stored in `module_flags` and `setModule` refuses to disable it, so a tenant can never lock itself out of administration. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `tenant.manage` permission | Added a new CORE-module permission `tenant.manage` (PLATFORM scope) for Vendor provisioning + module toggles; excluded from every tenant role (incl. Super Admin) via `NON_TENANT_KEYS`. Granted to Vendor Owner (PLATFORM). | confirm new key |
| 2026-06-05 | Provisioning is atomic + links existing users | `provisionTenant` runs in one `runAsPlatform` tx (tenant→flags→roles→Super Admin→assignment); a person can be Super Admin of multiple Khundis, so an existing OMJ-card holder is LINKED (not duplicated). Default tenant role catalog extracted to `src/provisioning/default-roles.ts` (one source for seed + provisioning). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Fixed latent step-4 seed bug | `seed.ts` referenced lowercase `RoleAltitude.platform/omj/tenant` (undefined under the `@kc/shared` enum); only survived because the seed runs via `ts-node --transpile-only` and no live DB ran it. Corrected to uppercase members. `prisma/*.ts` is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope — consider widening it later. | no (flagging) |
| — | Subdomain base | `{tenant}.khundiconnect.com` — **CONFIRMED/LOCKED** | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Login credential | **[DECIDE AT BUILD] → built BOTH:** OTP-to-phone as the default/primary (low-literacy, §13.2) AND a password fallback for users who set one. OTP is the recommended path. | yes (confirm OTP-primary is acceptable) |
| 2026-06-05 | Users are global (no RLS) | `users`/`sessions` carry **no `tenant_id` and no RLS** — they are platform-global identity; a single human holds stacked roles across tenants/altitudes (§5.5). Tenant/scope binding lives in `user_roles` (step 4). All access via the audited `runAsPlatform` path. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Authz tables are global (no RLS) | `permissions`/`roles`/`role_permissions`/`user_roles` carry **no RLS** — the engine must read a user's STACKED roles across every tenant + platform/omj altitudes to authorize one request (an ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM grant has null `tenant_context`; RLS-scoping would hide it and break cross-altitude authz). Read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path like `users`. **Tenant isolation is preserved by SCOPE resolution, not RLS on these tables**; every tenant-DATA table still uses the §-template RLS, and `tenants` RLS stays green (regression). `roles.tenant_id` is an ownership FK, not an isolation boundary. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module-enablement seam (step 4 vs 5) | Build-step 4 ships the dual-gate **guards**; the persistent `module_flags` table + Vendor toggle UI are build-step 5 (per §27). `ModuleEnablementService.isEnabled()` is default-open until step 5 backs it with `module_flags` (no tenant has a reduced plan yet); the GATE's blocking behaviour is proven now by tests. `core` (auth/roles/settings) is always-on/never-toggleable. Step 5 swaps the service body with NO guard/route change. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Scope reach model | Route scopes form a reach order OWN_TENANT<TENANT_SET<ALL_TENANTS<PLATFORM; a granted scope satisfies a required one if it provides ≥ reach for the target tenant (`scopeSatisfies`). PLATFORM routes need PLATFORM; ALL_TENANTS need ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM; single-tenant routes accept OWN_TENANT-anchored / TENANT_SET-containing / ALL_TENANTS / PLATFORM. Deny-by-default. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Role time-limit + IP restriction | Implemented from the schema: expired (`time_limited_until`) roles are skipped; a non-empty `ip_restrictions` array requires the requester IP to match (exact-match allow-list; **CIDR matching deferred** as a future enhancement). | confirm (CIDR scope) |
| 2026-06-05 | Session storage | Refresh **sessions persisted in Postgres** (`sessions` table) for durable rotation/revocation/reuse-detection; Redis used for ephemeral OTP + rate-limit. (§4 lists Redis for sessions; chose DB for refresh durability + testability.) | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Token transport | Access token (15m) returned in JSON body, held in memory by the SPA; refresh token (30d) only in an **httpOnly SameSite=Lax cookie** (Secure in prod). Two **distinct** JWT secrets required so a leaked access secret can't mint refresh tokens. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Password hashing | **Node `crypto` scrypt** (memory-hard, no native build dep) rather than bcrypt/argon2 — keeps gates runnable anywhere. Params encoded in the hash for future cost bumps. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Dev seed login users | 6 global identities seeded across altitudes (owner/OMJ/3 tenant admins/1 OTP-only member) with known OMJ card numbers; password users share a **dev-only fixture password** (env-overridable, dev/staging guard, NOT in this public file). Role assignment arrives in step 4. | no |
| — | Pricing (PKR) | [DECIDE AT BUILD] — placeholder tiers | yes |
| 2026-06-04 | Package manager | **npm workspaces** (not pnpm) so `deploy.sh` runs `npm ci` exactly per §28.6. `pnpm-workspace.yaml.disabled` documents this. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Foundation Prisma schema | **Model-free** (datasource+generator only). Tenant tables + RLS are deliberately deferred to build-step 2 so foundation defines no tenant data. `prisma generate` is a no-op until step 2. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Docker scope (step 1) | `docker-compose.yml` provisions dev **Postgres+Redis** (and CI service containers). App-process Dockerfiles deferred — VPS deploy path is **PM2**, not containers (§28.2); untested app images would add risk without value. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Node version (build env) | Target is **v22** (`.nvmrc`, engines `>=22`). This build/test ran on the sandbox's Node v24; `deploy.sh` warns (does not block) on version drift per §28.6. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS enforcement model | **GUC-based RLS** with `ENABLE` + `FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY`, keyed on transaction-local `app.current_tenant_id`; an explicit `app.bypass_rls='on'` GUC is the single audited cross-tenant path (§5.1). Single `DATABASE_URL` role for operator simplicity — **requires the app DB role to be non-superuser / no `BYPASSRLS`** (documented in `docs/MULTITENANCY.md` + `VPS_SETUP.md`), since superusers ignore RLS even with FORCE. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS test infrastructure | Isolation gate uses **PGlite** (Postgres compiled to WASM, in-process) so the test applies the *real* `migration.sql` and exercises genuine RLS with no Docker/superuser. Jest needs `--experimental-vm-modules` (PGlite loads WASM via dynamic import) — wired into the api `test` script. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Step-2 RLS demonstration table | RLS is proven on the **`tenants` registry itself** (a tenant session sees only its own row; cross-tenant read/write denied). The reusable per-table policy template (`tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`) is documented for every future tenant-scoped table; those tables + policies arrive with their own build-steps (members in step 6, etc.). | no |
| 2026-06-04 | turbo.json typecheck order | `typecheck` now `dependsOn ["^build","build"]` so Next.js's generated `.next/types` exist/are fresh before `tsc` (prevents a build/typecheck race). Build-tooling only; no runtime/live-path change. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Reserved subdomain labels | `www`, `staging`, `app`, `api`, `admin` resolve as platform entries (not tenants), so they can never be provisioned as a Khundi subdomain. | confirm list |

### Permanent build-correctness rules (deploy.sh / build config) — `feat/25-build-reliability`
Two deploy-blocking bugs were found on staging and fixed permanently (alongside the existing **prisma-generate-before-build** and **npm-ci-include-dev** rules). Both are now enforced by `deploy.sh` and asserted before PM2 restarts, and documented in ARCHITECTURE.md §28.5/§28.6 + docs/AUTH.md:

1. **API incremental-no-op trap.** `nest build` with `deleteOutDir:true` + `"incremental": true` (in `apps/api/tsconfig.json`) + a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` = an exit-0 build that wipes `dist/` then emits ZERO files, crashing the API with `Cannot find module './config/env.validation'`. **Fix:** removed `"incremental": true`; `deploy.sh` §5a now purges `*.tsbuildinfo`, `apps/api/dist`, and the turbo cache (`.turbo`, `node_modules/.cache/turbo`) before building; `turbo.json` build `outputs` include `dist/**` (no more "no output files found" warning). `deploy.sh` §5c asserts `apps/api/dist/main.js` AND `apps/api/dist/config/env.validation.js` exist, exiting non-zero otherwise so a broken build never restarts PM2.

2. **`NEXT_PUBLIC_*` not baked at build.** `next build` runs with `apps/web` as cwd and reads `.env` from the app dir (not the monorepo-root `.env`); turbo's strict env mode also strips undeclared vars. So a plain `turbo run build` did NOT inline `NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, silently killing the cross-subdomain login redirect (build-step 24) after deploy. **Fix:** `deploy.sh` §5b writes an explicit ALLOWLIST (`NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_OTP_LOGIN_ENABLED`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_MESSAGING_PROVIDER`) from the sourced `.env` into `apps/web/.env.local` before building; the same vars are declared in `turbo.json` build `env` for cache correctness. **Security:** the allowlist is the boundary — server secrets (`DATABASE_URL`, `JWT_*`, `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, `R2_*`) are NEVER copied. §5c greps `.next/static` to confirm the public value baked in (fail loudly if absent) AND scans for leaked secret values (abort if any found). Verified: clean API build emits `main.js`+`config/env.validation.js`; a plain web build bakes the domain into `.next/static`; no server secret appears in `.next/static`.
